       <script type="text/javascript">
        (function($){
             $(document).ready(function(){
                 function readCookie (name){
                     var nameEQ = name + "=";
                     var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
                     for(var i=0;i < ca.length;i++) {
                         var c = ca[i];
                         while (c.charAt(0)==' ') c = c.substring(1,c.length);
                         if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) == 0) return c.substring(nameEQ.length,c.length);
                     }
                     return null;
                 };
                 function isHomePage()
                 {
                     var url = window.location.href;
                     var domainPart = url;
                     if(url.indexOf("?") !== -1)
                     {
                         domainPart = url.split("?")[0];
                     }
                     domainPart = domainPart.replace(/\/$/, "");
                     return (window.location.origin === domainPart);
                 }
                 var FullBg = new function(){
                     this.container = null;
                     this.baseDelay = 0;
 
                     this.fadeIn = function(amount, duration){
                         this.container.animate({
                             opacity : amount
                         }, duration);
                         return this;
                     };
                     this.fadeOut = function(duration){
                         this.container.animate({
                             opacity : "0"
                         }, duration);
                         return this;
                     };
                     this.setTarget = function(elm){
                         if(elm)
                             this.container = elm;
                         return this;
                     };
                     this.closeBox = function(boxElm, duration){
                         this.setTarget(boxElm).fadeOut(duration);
                         return this;
                     };
                     this.destroy = function(elm){
                         elm.remove();
                         return this;
                     };
                     this.setAndRenderBoxSticky = function(linkElement, boxElement, positionName, duration){
                         duration = (duration) ? duration : 400;
                         var linkPagePosition = linkElement.position();
                         var linkPageOffset = linkElement.offset();
                         var boxElTop = linkPagePosition.top + linkElement.height();
                         var boxElLeft = (linkPageOffset.left + (linkElement.width()/2) - (boxElement.width())) + 25;
 
                         boxElement.css({
                             top: boxElTop,
                             left: boxElLeft,
                             position: positionName
                         });
 
                         elmCloned.fadeIn(duration);
                     };
 
                     this.setAndRenderBoxFixed = function(linkElement, boxElement, positionName, duration){
                         duration = (duration) ? duration : 400;
                         var linkPageOffset = linkElement.offset();
                         var boxElTop = linkPageOffset.top + linkElement.height();
                         var boxElLeft = (linkPageOffset.left + (linkElement.width()/2) - (boxElement.width())) + 25;
 
                         boxElement.css({
                             top: boxElTop,
                             left: boxElLeft,
                             position: positionName
                         });
 
                         elmCloned.fadeIn(duration);
                     }
                 };
 
                 var boxEl = $(".order-tracking-notif");
                 var customerType = readCookie("customerType");
 
                 if( isHomePage() && (typeof customerType === 'string' && customerType === 'returning') )
                 {
 
                     var isNotifShown = readCookie("itemTrackingNotif");
 
                     if(typeof isNotifShown !== 'string' || isNotifShown !== 'shown')
                     {
                         var headerEl = $(".header-main-wrapper");
                         var elmOriginal = $(".order-tracking-notif-box");
                         var linkEl = $(".order-tracking-header-main-href");
                         elmOriginal.clone().attr("data-sticky-ness", 'fixed').prependTo("body");
                         var elmCloned = $(".order-tracking-notif-box[data-sticky-ness='fixed']");
                         elmOriginal.remove();
                         FullBg.setAndRenderBoxFixed(linkEl, elmCloned, 'absolute', 500);
                         var headerAttrObserver = new MutationObserver(function(mutations){
                             var mutationObject = mutations[0];
                             if(mutationObject.attributeName === 'class')
                             {
                                 if($(mutationObject.target).hasClass("sticky"))
                                 {
                                     FullBg.setAndRenderBoxSticky(linkEl, elmCloned, 'fixed', 500);
                                 }
                                 else
                                 {
                                     FullBg.setAndRenderBoxFixed(linkEl, elmCloned, 'absolute', 500);
                                 }
 
                             }
                         });
 
                         headerAttrObserver.observe(headerEl.get(0), { attributes : true});
 
                         var fullBg = '<div id="order-tracking-notifc-full-bg"></div>';
                         $("body").prepend(fullBg);
 
                         var el = $("#order-tracking-notifc-full-bg");
 
                         FullBg.setTarget(el).fadeIn(0.5, 500);
                         FullBg.setTarget($(".order-tracking-notif")).fadeIn(1, 500);
 
                         var domainName = window.location.origin.replace("http://", "");
                         domainName = domainName.replace("https://", "");
                         document.cookie =
                                 'itemTrackingNotif=shown; domain=' + domainName + '; expires=3 Aug 2050 00:00:00 UTC; path=/';
 
                         $("body").on("click", ".order-tracking-notif, #order-tracking-notifc-full-bg", function(event){
                             try {
                                 event.preventDefault();
                                 FullBg.closeBox(boxEl, 500);
                                 FullBg.setTarget(el).fadeOut(600);
                                 FullBg.destroy(boxEl);
                                 FullBg.destroy(el);
 
                                 if ($(event.target).attr("id") === 'order-tracking-notif-btn-well') {
 
                                     window.location.href = $(event.target).attr("href");
                                 }
                                 else {
                                     elmCloned.fadeOut(500);
                                     elmCloned.remove();
                                 }
                             }
                             catch(e)
                             {
                                 FullBg.destroy(boxEl);
                                 FullBg.destroy(el);
                                 elmCloned.remove();
                                 if(headerAttrObserver)
                                 {
                                     headerAttrObserver.disconnect();
                                 }
                             }
                         });
 
                     }
                     else
                     {
                         FullBg.destroy(boxEl);
                         if(headerAttrObserver)
                         {
                             headerAttrObserver.disconnect();
                         }
                     }
                 }
                 else
                 {
                     FullBg.destroy(boxEl);
                 }
 
             });
         })(window.jQuery);
       </script>

                         <script>
                          $(document).ready(function () {
         $(".navigation-bar > .container >nav> .menu > li > div > .submenu").menuAim({
             activate: activateSubmenu,
             deactivate: deactivateSubmenu
         });
 
         function activateSubmenu(row) {
             var $row = $(row),
                 $submenu = $row.find("div.popover");
 
             $submenu.stop(true, true).show();
 
             $row.find("a").addClass("maintainHover");
         }
 
         function deactivateSubmenu(row) {
             var $row = $(row),
                 $submenu = $row.find("div.popover");
 
             $submenu.css("display", "none");
             $row.find("a").removeClass("maintainHover");
             $row.removeClass("default");
         }
 
         $(".submenu li").click(function (e) {
             e.stopPropagation();
         });
     });
                         </script>
                        </div>
                       </li>
                      </div>
                      <script type="text/javascript">
                       (function($){
         var usf = document.getElementById("_uf");
         $("#login-button-single").on("click", function(event){
             event.preventDefault();
         });
         if(usf && parseInt(usf.getAttribute("value"))===0)
         {
             var account =  document.getElementById("account");
             if(account)
             {
                 account.remove();
             }
         }
         else
         {
             var loginMenu =  document.getElementById("login-button-single");
             if(loginMenu)
             {
                 loginMenu.remove();
             }
 
             var account =  document.getElementById("account");
             if(account)
             {
                 var label = account.querySelector("[data-js-store='headerInfo.customer.label']");
                 label.innerHTML = label.innerHTML.replace("،");
             }
         }
     })(window.jQuery);
                      </script>

                        ScarabQueue = ScarabQueue || [];
             window.RecommendationBoxes = window.RecommendationBoxes || [];
             window.RecommendationLoadingFinished = false;
             window.RecommendationXhrSuccessfullCalls = 0;
             window.faultyBoxes = [];
             function number_format(number, decimals, dec_point, thousands_sep) {
                 var n = !isFinite(+number) ? 0 : +number,
                     prec = !isFinite(+decimals) ? 0 : Math.abs(decimals),
                     sep = (typeof thousands_sep === 'undefined') ? ',' : thousands_sep,
                     dec = (typeof dec_point === 'undefined') ? '.' : dec_point,
                     toFixedFix = function (n, prec) {
                         // Fix for IE parseFloat(0.55).toFixed(0) = 0;
                         var k = Math.pow(10, prec);
                         return Math.round(n * k) / k;
                     },
                     s = (prec ? toFixedFix(n, prec) : Math.round(n)).toString().split('.');
                 if (s[0].length > 3) {
                     s[0] = s[0].replace(/\B(?=(?:\d{3})+(?!\d))/g, sep);
                 }
                 if ((s[1] || '').length < prec) {
                     s[1] = s[1] || '';
                     s[1] += new Array(prec - s[1].length + 1).join('0');
                 }
                 return s.join(dec);
             }
             var $numberOfBoxes = 3;
                         
             ScarabQueue.push(['recommend', {
                 logic: "HOME_0",
                 limit: 25,
                 containerId: "cont-recommendation_box-0",
                 templateId: "tpl-recommendation_box-0",
                 success: function (SC, render) {
                                         var priceCurrency = "ریال";
                     if ((typeof SC !== "object" || !SC.hasOwnProperty("page")) || (SC.page.products.length === 0)) {
                         window.faultyBoxes.push("#main-wrapper-recommendation_box-0");
                     }
                     else {
                         var words_limit_for_title = 9;
                         for (var w = 0; w < SC.page.products.length; w++) {
                             var new_shortened_title = [];
                             var _title = SC.page.products[w].title;
                             var _wordsArray = _title.split(" ");
                             if (_wordsArray.length > words_limit_for_title) {
                                 for (var q = 0; q < words_limit_for_title - 1; q++) {
                                     new_shortened_title.push(_wordsArray[q]);
                                 }
                                 _title = new_shortened_title.join(" ") + "...";
                             }
                             SC.page.products[w].title = _title;
                             if( SC.page.products[w].price !== SC.page.products[w].msrp)
                             {
                                 var _price = "<span>" + number_format(SC.page.products[w].price, 0, "", ",") + "</span><span style='font-size: 11px;'>" + priceCurrency + "</span>";
                                 var _msrp = "<span style='text-decoration: line-through;'>"+number_format(SC.page.products[w].msrp, 0, "", ",") + "</span><span style='font-size: 11px;'>" + priceCurrency + "</span>";
 
                                 SC.page.products[w].price_tpl = "<p data-pricetype=\"current\">" + _price + "</div>";
                                 SC.page.products[w].price_tpl += "<p data-pricetype=\"original\">" + _msrp + "</div>";
 
                             }
                             else
                             {
                                 var _price =  "";
                                 var _msrp =  "<span>"+number_format(SC.page.products[w].msrp, 0, "", ",") + "</span><span style='font-size: 11px;'>" + priceCurrency + "</span>";
 
                                 SC.page.products[w].price_tpl = "<p data-pricetype=\"current\">" + _msrp + "</div>";
                             }
 
                         }
                     }

                     /**
                      * Creating a stack.
                      * Keeping the track of each box.
                      * We use this push & pop structure to delegate the creation of the carousels to
                      * window.onload; doing this, we ensure the execution of carousels when the resource is ready.
                      */
                     window.RecommendationBoxes.push({
                         element: "#cont-recommendation_box-0",
                         controls: "#carousel-ctrl-recommendation_box-0"
                     });
 
                     window.RecommendationXhrSuccessfullCalls++;
                                         var owlConfiguration = {
                         items: 5,
                         margin: 10,
                         loop: true,
                         rtl: true,
                         callbacks: true,
                         dots: false,
                         slideBy: 5,
                         nav: true,
                         navText: ["<div><img src=\"https://img.bamilo.com/ui/icon/hp/arrow.png\" /></div>",
                             "<div><img src=\"https://img.bamilo.com/ui/icon/hp/arrow.png\" /></div>"],
                         stagePadding: 40,
                         onChanged: function(obj){
                             if(obj && obj.hasOwnProperty("relatedTarget") && obj.relatedTarget.hasOwnProperty("$element"))
                             {
                                 obj.relatedTarget.$element.find(".each-box-product").removeClass("each-box-product-hidden");
                             }
                         },
                     };
                     if (window.RecommendationXhrSuccessfullCalls === $numberOfBoxes) {
                         if (window.jQuery().owlCarousel) {
                             for (var boxIncr = 0; boxIncr < window.RecommendationBoxes.length; boxIncr++) {
                                 $(window.RecommendationBoxes[boxIncr].element).show();
                                 var baseDur = 300;
                                 var i = 0;
                                 $(window.RecommendationBoxes[boxIncr].element).find(".each-box-product").each(function () {
                                     $(this).fadeIn(baseDur + (150 * i));
                                     i++;
                                 });
 
                                 owlConfiguration.navContainer = $(window.RecommendationBoxes[boxIncr].controls);
                                 $(window.RecommendationBoxes[boxIncr].element).owlCarousel(owlConfiguration);
 
                                 var _loader = $(window.RecommendationBoxes[boxIncr].element).siblings(".osh-spinner");
                                 if (_loader.length) {
                                     _loader.remove();
                                 }
                             }
                         }
                         else {

                                 for (var boxIncr = 0; boxIncr < window.RecommendationBoxes.length; boxIncr++) {
                                     $(window.RecommendationBoxes[boxIncr].element).show();

                                 }

                 templateId: "tpl-recommendation_box-2",
                 success: function (SC, render) {
                                         var priceCurrency = "ریال";
                     if ((typeof SC !== "object" || !SC.hasOwnProperty("page")) || (SC.page.products.length === 0)) {
                         window.faultyBoxes.push("#main-wrapper-recommendation_box-2");
                     }
                     else {
                         var words_limit_for_title = 9;
                         for (var w = 0; w < SC.page.products.length; w++) {
                             var new_shortened_title = [];
                             var _title = SC.page.products[w].title;
                             var _wordsArray = _title.split(" ");
                             if (_wordsArray.length > words_limit_for_title) {
                                 for (var q = 0; q < words_limit_for_title - 1; q++) {
                                     new_shortened_title.push(_wordsArray[q]);
                                 }
                                 _title = new_shortened_title.join(" ") + "...";
                             }
                             SC.page.products[w].title = _title;
                             if( SC.page.products[w].price !== SC.page.products[w].msrp)
                             {
                                 var _price = "<span>" + number_format(SC.page.products[w].price, 0, "", ",") + "</span><span style='font-size: 11px;'>" + priceCurrency + "</span>";
                                 var _msrp = "<span style='text-decoration: line-through;'>"+number_format(SC.page.products[w].msrp, 0, "", ",") + "</span><span style='font-size: 11px;'>" + priceCurrency + "</span>";
 
                                 SC.page.products[w].price_tpl = "<p data-pricetype=\"current\">" + _price + "</div>";
                                 SC.page.products[w].price_tpl += "<p data-pricetype=\"original\">" + _msrp + "</div>";
 
                             }
                             else
                             {
                                 var _price =  "";
                                 var _msrp =  "<span>"+number_format(SC.page.products[w].msrp, 0, "", ",") + "</span><span style='font-size: 11px;'>" + priceCurrency + "</span>";
 
                                 SC.page.products[w].price_tpl = "<p data-pricetype=\"current\">" + _msrp + "</div>";
                             }
 
                         }
                     }
 
 
                     render(SC);
 
                     $("#cont-recommendation_box-2").addClass("bordered-left");
 
                     /**
                      * Creating a stack.
                      * Keeping the track of each box.
                      * We use this push & pop structure to delegate the creation of the carousels to
                      * window.onload; doing this, we ensure the execution of carousels when the resource is ready.
                      */
                     window.RecommendationBoxes.push({
                         element: "#cont-recommendation_box-2",
                         controls: "#carousel-ctrl-recommendation_box-2"
                     });
 
                     window.RecommendationXhrSuccessfullCalls++;
                                         var owlConfiguration = {
                         items: 5,
                         margin: 10,
                         loop: true,
                         rtl: true,
                         callbacks: true,
                         dots: false,
                         slideBy: 5,
                         nav: true,
                         navText: ["<div><img src=\"https://img.bamilo.com/ui/icon/hp/arrow.png\" /></div>",
                             "<div><img src=\"https://img.bamilo.com/ui/icon/hp/arrow.png\" /></div>"],
                         stagePadding: 40,
                         onChanged: function(obj){
                             if(obj && obj.hasOwnProperty("relatedTarget") && obj.relatedTarget.hasOwnProperty("$element"))
                             {
                                 obj.relatedTarget.$element.find(".each-box-product").removeClass("each-box-product-hidden");
                             }
                         },
                     };
                     if (window.RecommendationXhrSuccessfullCalls === $numberOfBoxes) {
                         if (window.jQuery().owlCarousel) {
                             for (var boxIncr = 0; boxIncr < window.RecommendationBoxes.length; boxIncr++) {
                                 $(window.RecommendationBoxes[boxIncr].element).show();
                                 var baseDur = 300;
                                 var i = 0;
                                 $(window.RecommendationBoxes[boxIncr].element).find(".each-box-product").each(function () {
                                     $(this).fadeIn(baseDur + (150 * i));
                                     i++;
                                 });
 
                                 owlConfiguration.navContainer = $(window.RecommendationBoxes[boxIncr].controls);
                                 $(window.RecommendationBoxes[boxIncr].element).owlCarousel(owlConfiguration);
 
                                 var _loader = $(window.RecommendationBoxes[boxIncr].element).siblings(".osh-spinner");
                                 if (_loader.length) {
                                     _loader.remove();
                                 }
                             }
                         }
                         else {
                             window.addEventListener("load", function () {
                                 for (var boxIncr = 0; boxIncr < window.RecommendationBoxes.length; boxIncr++) {
                                     $(window.RecommendationBoxes[boxIncr].element).show();
                                     var baseDur = 300;
                                     var i = 0;
                                     $(window.RecommendationBoxes[boxIncr].element).find(".each-box-product").each(function () {
                                         $(this).fadeIn(baseDur + (150 * i));
                                         i++;
                                     });
                                     owlConfiguration.navContainer = $(window.RecommendationBoxes[boxIncr].controls);
                                     $(window.RecommendationBoxes[boxIncr].element).owlCarousel(owlConfiguration);
 
                                     var _loader = $(window.RecommendationBoxes[boxIncr].element).siblings(".osh-spinner");
                                     if (_loader.length) {
                                         _loader.remove();
                                     }
                                 }
                             });
                         }
 
                     }
                                         if (faultyBoxes.length) {
                         for (var g = 0; g < faultyBoxes.length; g++) {
                             $(faultyBoxes[g]).hide();
                         }
                     }
                 }
             }]);
                       </script>
                       <script type="text/javascript">
                        function shortenImage(path)
         {
             var rule = new RegExp(/\.(jpg|jpeg|png)$/);
             return path.replace(rule, "-catalog.$1");
         }
         function shortenTitle(title)
         {
             return title;
         }
                       </script>
